int f(int a, int b) {
    return a + b;

    x = f(5);

program34.c

Lexer: OK Parser: OK
Source Code 
int main(void) {
    int x;
    for (x = 0; x < 10; x = x + 1) {
        int y;
        y = 5;
    }
    y = 10;
    return y;
}

int main(void) {
    float value;
    int *pointer;
    value = 1.0;
    pointer = &value;
    return *pointer;
}
